Lets indulge xx  \nLine Up \nANDRAS \nPeel back the leaves and discover Andrs, a Melbourne producer making tactile and imperfect electronic music. Inspired by primitive percussion, simple melodies and home recording, Andras combines elements of house music and new age ambience in a distinctly antipodean way. Based around drum machine rhythms and new age synths, his original tape recordings are simultaneously contemporary in sound and difficult to carbon date, slipping comfortably between Library Music, 90s House and instrumental synth funk. Presenting the weekly radio show Strange Holiday on 3RRR FM in Melbourne has given him a chance to greatly expand his record collection, which currently occupies the broad territory between Disco, World, Library and Balearic sounds. This depth of knowledge about musics past informs his productions, which all give a nod and a wink to the past. Andrs has supported artists including James Pants, Andres & DJ Sprinkles, as well as recently returning from an extended EU tour. Were proud to be hosting this world class DJ and producer for his first Trust appearance. \nSILVERSIX \nSilversix is a producer & DJ based in Melbourne, Australia. His production has enjoyed building success over the years with countless originals and remixes. Hes officially remixed for some of the biggest in the business, including names like Nile Rodgers, Booka Shade, Jos Gonzlez to name a few As a DJ, hes headlined countless institutions around the country, played at a long list of festivals & events as well as holding a high number of DJ residencies in his career. Hes a feature resident at the infamous Revolver Sundays, playing alongside the best DJs in the country and supporting such internationals as Andhim, Nice7, Amine Edge, Tube & Berger, Pleasurekraft, Round Table Knights, DJ PP, Monkey Safari and Robosonic. Silversix has taken his DJing and production to a new level in recent times, catching the eye of the Trust head chefs with his impeccable track selection and flawless mixing. Silversix is DJs DJ, capable of matching it with the very best on the international circuit. \nRETZA \nTake a minute to get acquainted with Retza, a man as humble as he is talented and one of Melbournes most sought-after and respected DJs and Producers. Retza will be showcasing some of his fresh productions, as well as some tunes that are stroking his beard at the moment.
